***забраковать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забраковать.html>забракова́ть</a> (19676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:браковать.html>бракова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brakovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забраковать.html>забракова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabrakovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:браковать.html>бракова́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">забрако́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reject, to consider defective</li>
<li>to condemn</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zabordlo</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">заборо́ло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaborólo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.

***забрасывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a> (13849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabrósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabrásyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw, to cast, to hurl <i>(somewhere)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корзина.html>корзи́ну</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баскетбол.html>баскетбо́ле</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrásyvatʹ</b> mjač v korzínu (v basketbóle)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw the ball into the basket</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to send
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrásyvatʹ</b> desánt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drop a landing force</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разведчик.html>разве́дчика</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тыл.html>тыл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrásyvatʹ</b> razvédčika v tyl protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">send a spy deep into the enemy rear</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take <i>(to a place)</i></li>
<li>to put, to mislay</li>
<li>to neglect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrásyvatʹ</b> rabótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to neglect one's work</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give up, to drop</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zakídyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabrosátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabrásyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pelt <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>камня́ми</a> кого́-либо (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>дре́внем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́нии</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:осуждать.html>осужда́ть</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrásyvatʹ</b> kamnjámi kovó-libo (o drévnem nakazánii; osuždátʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stone smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зью</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrásyvatʹ</b> grjázʹju kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sling mud at smb; drag smb through the dirt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shower <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цвета́ми</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рками</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrásyvatʹ</b> cvetámi (podárkami)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shower with flowers (presents)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrásyvatʹ</b> kovó-libo voprósami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pelt/bombard smb with questions</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fill <i>(with)</i>, to fill up <i>(with)</i>, to cover <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́му</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:песок.html>песко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrásyvatʹ</b> jámu peskóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill (up) a hole with sand</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zakídyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***забрать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забрать.html>забра́ть</a> (1621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрать.html>забра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take away, to seize, to collect; to capture, to take possession
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрать.html>забра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrátʹ</b> sebé v gólovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take it into one's head</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to collect, to pick up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрать.html>забра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrátʹ</b> továr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pick up the goods</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to arrest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>людьми́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приезжать.html>приезжа́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́нах</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:называемый.html>называ́емых</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:воронко.html>воро́нках</a>», <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ноча́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лыми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:семья.html>се́мьями</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Za ljudʹmí prijezžáli na čórnyx mašínax, tak nazyvájemyx “vorónkax”, po nočám i <b>zabiráli</b> célymi sémʹjami.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They came for people in black cars, the so-called "voronkas" ("paddy wagons") in the night and <b>arrested</b> entire families.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pick up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to collect a passenger</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сы́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>zabiráju</b> sýna pósle rabóty.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I pick up (my) son after work.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bear, to turn off, to turn aside
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забрать.html>забра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вправо.html>впра́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrátʹ</b> vprávo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bear (to the) right</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***забрезжить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забрезжить.html>забре́зжить</a> (21235)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезжить.html>бре́зжить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brézžitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрезжить.html>забре́зжить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabrézžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брезжить.html>бре́зжить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin to dawn</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брести.html>брести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***забросать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a> (20114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросать.html>броса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brosátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabrosátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pelt <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a></b> чью́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>камня́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrosátʹ</b> čʹjú-libo mašínu kamnjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pelt smb's car with stones</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>камня́ми</a> кого́-либо (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>дре́внем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́нии</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:осуждать.html>осужда́ть</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrosátʹ</b> kamnjámi kovó-libo (o drévnem nakazánii; osuždátʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stone smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зью</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrosátʹ</b> grjázʹju kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sling mud at smb; drag smb through the dirt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shower <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цвета́ми</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рками</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrosátʹ</b> cvetámi (podárkami)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shower with flowers (presents)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrosátʹ</b> kovó-libo voprósami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pelt/bombard smb with questions</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:жалоба.html>жа́лобами</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">menjá <b>zabrosáli</b> rabótoj (žálobami)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am snowed under with work (complaints)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fill <i>(with)</i>, to fill up <i>(with)</i>, to cover <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросать.html>заброса́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́му</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:песок.html>песко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrosátʹ</b> jámu peskóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill (up) (cover) a hole with sand</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***забросить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сить</a> (3544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросить.html>бро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabrósitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрасывать.html>забра́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw, to cast, to hurl <i>(somewhere)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корзина.html>корзи́ну</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баскетбол.html>баскетбо́ле</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrósitʹ</b> mjač v korzínu (v basketbóle)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw the ball into the basket</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to send
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrósitʹ</b> desánt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drop a landing force</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разведчик.html>разве́дчика</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тыл.html>тыл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrósitʹ</b> razvédčika v tyl protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">send a spy deep into the enemy rear</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьба́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сила</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> (куда́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sudʹbá <b>zabrósila</b> jevó (kudá-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fate brought him (to a place); he found himself (at a place)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take <i>(to a place)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́шу</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ге</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja vam <b>zabróšu</b> éto po doróge</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'll drop it off at your place on my way</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put, to mislay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сил</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шляпа.html>шля́пу</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kudá ty <b>zabrósil</b> šljápu?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">where did you put the hat?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrósitʹ</b> nógu na nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cross one's legs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to neglect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabrósitʹ</b> rabótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to neglect one's work</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершенно.html>соверше́нно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заброшенный.html>забро́шены</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">déti soveršénno zabróšeny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the children are completely neglected</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give up, to drop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забросить.html>забро́сил</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:занятие.html>заня́тия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>zabrósil</b> zanjátija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has given up [dropped] his studies</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zakínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***забрызгать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забрызгать.html>забры́згать</a> (15361)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брызгать.html>бры́згать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brýzgatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрызгать.html>забры́згать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabrýzgatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брызгать.html>бры́згать</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to splatter, to begin to splash</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрызгать.html>забры́згать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabrýzgatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брызгать.html>бры́згать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">забры́згивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sprinkle (someone with liquid)</li>

***забулькать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забулькать.html>забу́лькать</a> (29455)</h1><br><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:булькать.html>бу́лькать</a> n class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Чтоб не дать слабину, он зажал его пальцами, кровь <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">забулькала</span> в горле, он попробовал сплюнуть ее, а она улучила момент и опять побежала по пальцам и по губам. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>
</body>

***забываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́ться</a> (9509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забывать.html>забыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabyvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забыться.html>забы́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to doze, to drop off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лёг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забыться.html>забы́лся</a></b>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">perfective</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On ljóg i <b>zabýlsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He lay down and dropped off.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become oblivious, to lose contact with reality
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́юсь</a></b>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́юсь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вине́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I <b>zabyvájusʹ</b>, <b>zabyvájusʹ</b> ja v viné.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And I become oblivious in wine. (from a song)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to forget oneself, to cross the line of what is allowed or to lose control over oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молодо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́йтесь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Molodój čelovék, ne <b>zabyvájtesʹ</b>, vy ne dóma!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Young man, don't <b>forget yourself</b>, you are not at home!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забывать.html>забыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́ются</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nóvyje slová býstro <b>zabyvájutsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">New words <b>are/get forgotten</b> quickly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***забывающийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забываться.html>забыва́ющийся</a> (9509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
